A proxy statement with further information regarding the 2022 Annual Meeting will be distributed to stockholders prior to such meeting.</span></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:4.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><span style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;">Deadline for Rule 14a-8 Stockholder Proposals</span></p>
  <p style="text-indent:4.533%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:4.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><span style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">Under the Securities and Exchange Commission&#x2019;s proxy rules, the Company has set the deadline for submission of proposals to be included in the proxy materials for the 2022 Annual Meeting as April 8, 2022. Accordingly, in order for a stockholder proposal to be considered for inclusion in the Company&#x2019;s proxy materials for the 2022 Annual Meeting, the proposal must be received by the Company at 35 Cambridgepark Drive, Cambridge, Massachusetts 02140, Attention: Corporate Secretary, on or before April 8, 2022, and comply with the procedures and requirements set forth in Rule 14a-8 under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934.</span></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:4.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><span style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;">Advance Notice Deadline for Director Nominations and Other Stockholder Proposals</span></p>
  <p style="text-indent:4.533%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:4.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><span style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">In accordance with the Company&#x2019;s Bylaws, for director nominations or stockholder proposals to be brought before the 2022 Annual Meeting, other than Rule 14a-8 proposals described above, written notice must be received by the Company at 35 Cambridgepark Drive, Cambridge, Massachusetts 02140, Attention: Corporate Secretary no later than April 8, 2022. Such notices must also comply with the requirements of the Company&#x2019;s Bylaws and other applicable law.</span></p>

  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:right;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">Exhibit 99.1</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Pyxis Oncology Provides Corporate and Financial Update</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:4.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">Announces Expansion of Novel Immuno-Oncology Therapeutic Portfolio with Addition of Anti-Siglec-15 In-licensed from Biosion (PYX-106)</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:4.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> Introduces First Internally Developed IO Candidate Anti-KLRG1 (PYX-102)</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:4.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">Cash Runway Sufficient for Multiple Milestones Through Third Quarter 2024</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:4.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">Company to Host Conference Call and Webcast Today at 8:00 a.m. ET</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:14.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">CAMBRIDGE, Mass., March 29, 2022</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> &#x2013; Pyxis Oncology, Inc. (Nasdaq: PYXS), a multi-asset, multi-modality company focused on developing next-generation therapeutics for difficult to treat cancers, today provided a corporate and financial update and reported financial results for the full year ended December 31, 2021.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#x201c;We have had a highly productive start to 2022, advancing our lead programs toward first-in-human clinical trials while executing our strategy of identifying the most promising scientific breakthroughs and therapeutics in the treatment of cancers,&#x201d; said Lara Sullivan, M.D., Chief Executive Officer of Pyxis Oncology. &#x201c;The in-licensing of Biosion&#x2019;s anti-Siglec-15 (PYX-106) and the introduction of our first internally developed candidate anti-KLRG1 (PYX-102) further validate our approach to portfolio and pipeline expansion by identifying and progressing some of the most promising scientific and clinical advances from either our internal discovery engines or external sources.&#x201d;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#x201c;We are excited to partner with Pyxis Oncology and its experienced management team for the development of this promising asset,&#x201d; said Hugh M. Davis, Ph.D., Chief Operating Officer, Biosion, Inc. and President, Biosion USA, Inc. &#x201c;While immunotherapies have improved the lives of many patients, only a fraction respond to treatment, suggesting that our understanding of how cancer is able to evade the immune system is incomplete. We believe that anti-Siglec-15 may represent a breakthrough and that targeting siglec-15 could extend the benefits of immunotherapies to broader patient populations, including those who have failed PD-(L)1 targeting therapies.&#x201d;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:14.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Corporate Development Highlights</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">License agreement with Biosion adds anti-Siglec-15 to Pyxis Oncology&#x2019;s IO pipeline</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">: Pyxis Oncology announced today it has in-licensed anti-Siglec-15,now referred to as PYX-106, a potentially best-in-class monoclonal antibody which is a novel immune checkpoint. In pre-clinical studies, PYX-106 is broadly expressed across a range of solid tumors among difficult-to-treat cancers.  The American Academy for Cancer Research (AACR) has accepted an abstract submitted by Biosion for PYX-106. The poster will be made available at the start of the AACR Annual Meeting on April 8, 2022. Pyxis Oncology expects to file an IND for PYX-106 in the second half of 2022.  </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Pipeline expansion with the addition of Company&#x2019;s first internally developed candidate</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">: Pyxis Oncology announced today the declaration of its first internally developed candidate, an anti-KLRG1 monoclonal antibody program now referred to as PYX-102. PYX-102 originated as part of the Company&#x2019;s proprietary IO target catalog and work out of Pyxis Oncology founder Tom Gajewski&#x2019;s lab at the University of Chicago. The Company expects to provide further updates closer to the planned IND submission for PYX-102 in the second half of 2023. </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Additional GLP study underway for PYX-202</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">:  Pyxis Oncology&#x2019;s anti-DLK1 ADC, PYX-202</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">, </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">was licensed in from LegoChem Biosciences, Inc. in December 2020.  In preparation for an IND filing and based on observation of the Company&#x2019;s GLP studies to date, management has decided to conduct additional GLP and non-GLP toxicity studies to determine whether PYX-202 is a viable clinical candidate. The Company will continue to monitor the progress of its PYX-202 program and expects to provide an update about PYX-202 in mid-2022.</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Advancing programs toward the clinic with near-term catalysts</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">: Pyxis Oncology expects to file INDs for anti-EDB, PYX-201, and anti-CD123, PYX-203, in the second half of 2022 and in the second half of 2023, respectively. </font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">1</font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:14.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Financial Update</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">As of March 29, 2022, Pyxis Oncology had cash and cash equivalents of approximately $253 million (preliminary, unaudited), </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">which is expected to fund operations into the third quarter of 2024. </font></div></div>
  <p style="margin-left:9.067%;text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#x201c;</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">With a solid balance sheet and cash runway sufficient to deliver multiple catalysts through the third quarter of 2024, we remain focused on building and advancing our pipeline through a multi-asset, multi-modality approach that we believe will unlock benefits for patients,&#x201d; said Pam Connealy, Chief Financial Officer.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Research and development </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">expenses for the full year ended December 31, 2021 were $51.1 million, compared to $9.1 million for the full year ended December 31, 2020. The increase in research and development expenses was primarily attributed to increased expenses associated with the addition of three antibody-drug conjugates to the Company&#x2019;s portfolio and an increase in employee headcount to support research and development activities. </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">General and administrative expenses for the full year ended December 31, 2021 were $18.6 million, compared to $3.8 million for the year ended December 31, 2020. The increase was primarily attributed to higher personnel-related expenses (including stock-based compensation), and costs incurred to support the growth and expansion of the business, overhead and facilities. </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Net loss for the full year ended December 31, 2021 was </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">$76.0 million ($8.95 per common share), compared to $12.8 million ($12.45 per common share) for the year ended December 31, 2020. The increase in net loss is primarily attributed to the addition of three antibody-drug conjugates to the Company&#x2019;s portfolio and the Company&#x2019;s preparations to initiate human clinical trials for PYX-201.</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.528%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:4.537%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:4.7521786492374725%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">As of March 25, 2022, the outstanding number of shares of Common Stock of Pyxis Oncology was 32,841,747.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:14.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Conference Call and Webcast Details</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Pyxis Oncology management will host a conference call and live webcast on Tuesday, March 29, 2022, at 8:00 a.m. ET to discuss recent corporate updates. The live call can be accessed by dialing (833) 945-2461 (domestic) or (520) 809-9726 (international) using the conference ID 5458057. A live webcast can be accessed at </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">https://edge.media-server.com/mmc/p/c8uwd9dr</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> or on the Investors section of the Pyxis Oncology website at </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">ir.pyxisoncology.com</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">. A replay of the webcast will be available approximately two hours after completion of the call and will be archived on the Company&#x2019;s website for up to 45 days.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">About Pyxis Oncology, Inc.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.2649999999999997;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Pyxis Oncology, Inc. is a multi-asset multi-modality company focused on defeating difficult to treat cancers</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> and improving patient lives. By leveraging our fully integrated research, development and commercial capabilities, our expert team is efficiently building a diversified portfolio of next-generation therapeutics. Pyxis Oncology&#x2019;s therapeutic candidates are designed to directly kill tumor cells, and to address the underlying pathologies created by cancer that enable its uncontrollable proliferation and immune evasion. Since its launch in 2019, Pyxis Oncology has developed a broad portfolio of novel antibody-drug conjugate product candidates, and monoclonal antibody, or mAb, preclinical discovery programs that it is developing as monotherapies and in combination with other therapies. To learn more about Pyxis Oncology, visit </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">www.pyxisoncology.com</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">2</font></p>
